*Tyler Bortel,Peter Moeck*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于信息论的新型算法，用于校正原子分辨率图像中的对称性破缺，并用石墨和二硫化钼的实验图像验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字晶体图像由于成像过程和晶体真实结构而必然存在对称性破缺，而算法校正对称性破缺可以纠正成像过程引入的许多失真。

Method: 通过数值量化恢复对称性来评估一种新的成像后校正方法的有效性，并采用信息论方法。

Result: 使用扫描隧道显微镜、原子力显微镜和像差校正透射电子显微镜获得的石墨和二硫化钼的13张实验原子分辨率图像被用作测试用例。

Conclusion: 新开发的信息论方法适用于校正原子分辨率图像中的对称性破缺，并且所使用的软件源代码和完整报告可在 GitHub 上公开获取。

Abstract: Digital images from crystals, as projected from the third spatial dimension
and recorded in atomic resolution with any kind of real-world microscope,
feature necessarily broken symmetries of the translation-periodicity-restricted
Euclidean plane. The symmetry breakings are due to both the imaging process and
the real structure of the imaged crystal, with the former cause typically
dominating. A posterior algorithmic reduction of the symmetry breaking in such
images constitutes, thus, often a correction for many of the distortions that
were introduced by the imaging processes. Numerically quantified restorations
of such symmetries can, therefore, be used to demonstrate the efficacy of a
newly implemented posterior correction method for atomic-resolution images from
hexagonal crystals. Recently developed information theory based methods are
here shown to be suitable for this purpose. Thirteen experimental
atomic-resolution images from graphite and monolayer molybdenite (MoS2), as
respectively obtained by scanning tunneling microscopy, atomic force microscopy
in the torsional resonance mode, and aberration-corrected parallel illumination
transmission electron microscopy served as test cases in our larger (in its
totality so far unpublished) study, from which we quote here. The source code
of the software that was used for our distortion corrections and the whole
report on that study are freely available on GitHub.

</details>


### [271] [Equivalence of charged and neutral density functional formulations for correcting the many-body self-interaction of polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02159)
*Stefano Falletta,Jennifer Coulter,Joel B. Varley,Daniel Aberg,Babak Sadigh,Boris Kozinsky,Alfredo Pasquarello*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 密度泛函理论中的电子自相互作用问题影响了极化子的准确模拟。本文证明了带电和中性密度泛函形式在处理极子状态的多体自相互作用时是等价的，并将分段线性泛函、pSIC 方法和极化子的单位晶胞方法联系起来。这些方法在形式上得到相同的自相互作用校正能量表达式，该表达式完全由带电极化子结构的其中性电荷态的能量学定义。在此基础上，我们对 MgO 中的空穴极化子、$eta$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ 中的空穴极化子、$V_	ext{k}$ 在 NaI 中、BiVO$_4$ 中的电子极化子和 TiO$_2$ 中的电子极化子进行了计算，结果表明两种形式的计算结果在基态性质上非常吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子自相互作用问题影响了密度泛函理论中极化子的准确模拟，现有的带电和中性密度泛函形式的定量关系尚不清楚。

Method: 本文通过连接分段线性泛函、pSIC 方法和单位晶胞方法，证明了带电和中性密度泛函形式在处理极子状态的多体自相互作用时是等价的，并推导了相同的自相互作用校正能量表达式。

Result: 通过对 MgO、$eta$-Ga$_2$O$_3$、NaI、BiVO$_4$ 和 TiO$_2$ 中的极化子进行计算，表明带电和中性密度泛函形式得到的基态性质结果非常吻合。

Conclusion: 带电和中性密度泛函形式在处理极化子问题时是等价的，它们之间的差异仅源于极化子结构的形成，而这又受电子筛选和有限尺寸效应处理方法的影响。

Abstract: The electron self-interaction problem in density functional theory affects
the accurate modeling of polarons, particularly their localization and
formation energy. Charged and neutral density functional formulations have been
developed to address this issue, yet their relationship remains unclear. Here,
we demonstrate their equivalence in treating the many-body self-interaction of
the polaron state. In particular, we connect with each other piecewise-linear
functionals based on adding an extra charge to the supercell, the pSIC approach
derived from the energetics of the neutral defect with polaronic distortions in
a supercell, and the unit-cell method for polarons based on electron-phonon
couplings. We show that these approaches lead to the same formal expression of
the self-interaction corrected energy, which is fully defined by the energetics
of the neutral charge state of the charged polaronic structure. Residual
differences between these methods solely arise from the achieved polaronic
structure, which is affected by different treatments of electron-screening and
finite-size effects. We apply these methods to a set of prototypical small hole
and electron polarons, including the hole polaron in MgO, the hole polaron in
$\beta$-Ga$_2$O$_3$, the $V_\text{k}$ center in NaI, the electron polaron in
BiVO$_4$, and the electron polaron in TiO$_2$. We show that the ground-state
properties of polarons obtained using charged and neutral density functional
formulations are in excellent agreement.

via solution processing remains challenging due to the precursor's low
solubility, and current additive or solvent engineering strategies are often
complex and poorly reproducible. High-pressure recrystallization has recently
emerged as a promising route to improve film quality, yet its impact on film
properties remains insufficiently explored. Here, we systematically investigate
the morphological, structural, and optical properties of CsPbBr$_3$ thin films
prepared by high-pressure recrystallization, in comparison with standard
non-recrystallized films. Optimized recrystallization at 300 bar produces
smooth, pinhole-free, single-phase 3D perovskite layers with sub-nanometer
roughness, while the film thickness is precisely tunable via precursor
concentration. The process enhances both grain and crystallite sizes, leading
to amplified spontaneous emission with a reduced excitation threshold and
improved photostability. Temperature-dependent X-ray diffraction further
reveals the orthorhombic--tetragonal--cubic phase transition, consistent with
single-crystal behavior. This study provides fundamental insights into
pressure-driven recrystallization and establishes a reproducible, scalable
approach for fabricating high-quality CsPbBr$_3$ films for optoelectronic

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The hybridization gap in strained-layer InAs/InxGa1-xSb quantum spin Hall

wells (QWs) be strained while still preserving the fundamental QSHI phase? In
this study, we demonstrate the controlled molecular beam epitaxial (MBE) growth

Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang (BHZ) model, confirming the preservation of topologically

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The structural, vibrational, and optical properties of Rb$_2$TeBr$_6$ have
been investigated under high pressure using synchrotron X-ray diffraction,
Raman spectroscopy, photoluminescence (PL), and optical absorption
measurements. At ambient conditions, Rb$_2$TeBr$_6$ crystallizes in the cubic
Fm-3m structure, which remains stable below 8.0 GPa. Within this pressure
range, subtle inter-octahedral rotations develop, producing a gradual localized
deviation from the ideal cubic framework. This local reorientation facilitates
radiative recombination, leading to a pronounced enhancement of PL intensity
with pressure up to 2.4 GPa. Beyond this pressure point, enhancement of
nonradiative relaxation channels result in gradual PL quenching. Additionally,
the PL intensity increases upon the application of an external weak magnetic
field. A structural transition to the orthorhombic Pnnm phase occurs at around
8.0 GPa, followed by a monoclinic P$2_1/m$ phase above 10.7 GPa, and eventual
amorphization beyond 25.5 GPa. Optical absorption spectra reveal continuous
band-gap narrowing upon compression. These findings demonstrate the strong
coupling among lattice dynamics, electronic structure, and optical response in
Rb$_2$TeBr$_6$, underscoring its potential as a pressure-tunable optoelectronic
material

Abstract: The planar Hall effect (PHE) is typically symmetric under magnetic field
reversal, as required by the Onsager reciprocity relations. Recent advances
have identified the antisymmetric PHE (under magnetic field reversal) as an
intriguing extension in magnetic systems. While new mechanisms have been
proposed, the role of conventional anisotropic magnetoresistance (AMR) in this
phenomenon remains unclear. Here, we report the experimental discovery of an

fourth-rank AMR tensor inherent to C3-symmetric planes, assisted by PMA. Our
findings link conventional AMR to antisymmetric galvanomagnetic responses,
offering new insights into symmetry-governed transport in crystalline
ferromagnets.

### [277] [Strain-Tunable Opto-electronics in PdS$_2$ Monolayer: the Role of Band Nesting and Carrier-Phonon Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02383)
*Hongfa Wang,Yancheng Gong,Subrahmanyam Pattamatta,Junwen Li,Hailong Wang,Zhizi Guan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用第一性原理计算和形变势理论。

Result: 二维PdS2单层材料在双轴拉伸应变下，光学吸收峰从~2.0 eV红移至~1.6 eV，电子迁移率增加超过三倍。光学响应归因于能带嵌套特性，载流子迁移率的提高与载流子有效质量减小和载流子-声子散射抑制有关。

Conclusion: 提出了一种通过工程应变来调控具有强能带嵌套特性的二维半导体材料的光电响应的途径，为设计可调谐的柔性光电器件提供了思路。

Abstract: Strain engineering is a powerful strategy for tuning the optoelectronic
properties in two-dimensional materials, yet the underlying mechanisms
governing their strain response are often not fully elucidated. In this work,
our first-principle calculations show that the penta-orthorhombic PdS$_2$

optical response originates from a robust band nesting feature between the
highest valence and lowest conduction bands, which is preserved across the
Brillouin zone under biaxial strain. For the carrier transport, deformation
potential theory predicts mobility increasing with strain, strongly correlating
with the reduction of carrier effective mass. Our first-principles calculations
show a strain-induced monotonic decrease in carrier linewidths near the band
edges, indicating suppressed carrier-phonon scattering and longer carrier
lifetime as the origin of the mobility enhancement. Our work establishes a
pathway for engineering the optoelectronic response in 2D semiconductors where
strong band nesting governs the optical properties and paves the way for the
rational design of continuously tunable flexible optoelectronic devices.

Abstract: Recently, altermagnets have emerged as promising candidates in spintronics,
uniquely combining large spin-polarized electronic states with zero net

further establish a way to prescreen altermagnet candidates that favor the

work elucidates the interplay between magnetic order and spin-orbit coupling in
governing spin polarization in altermagnet candidates, and thereby advances the
materials design paradigm for spin-functional devices.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 与块状半导体不同，纳米线中的空间限制会导致表面散射，从而降低载流子迁移率并破坏传统模型的空间均匀性假设。

Method: 开发了一个基于空间依赖性玻尔兹曼输运方程的从头算框架，并将其应用于具有扩散表面散射的硅和氮化镓纳米线，以揭示迁移率与直径的关系。

Result: 推导了纳米线迁移率与直径的关系式：$\mu_\mathrm{1D} = \mu_\mathrm{bulk} \left[1-\left(d/d_0\right)^{-\beta}\right]$。其中，$d_0$ 是与载流子平均自由程相当的特征长度，$eta$ 是一个与电子-声子散射和表面散射竞争相关的参数。此外，还讨论了取向、横截面形状和温度的影响。

Conclusion: 该理论方法可以为优化实验提供一个内在的基准，因为实验数据通常低于理论预测，这可能归因于结构缺陷和测量误差。

Abstract: Carrier mobility in bulk semiconductors is typically governed by
electron-phonon (e-ph) scattering. In nanostructures, spatial confinement can
lead to significant surface scattering, lowering mobility and breaking the
spatial homogeneity assumption of conventional models. In this work, a fully ab
initio framework based on the spatially dependent Boltzmann transport equation
for one-dimensional nanowires is developed. We apply it to Si and GaN assuming
diffusive surface scattering, and reveal the mobility-diameter relation:
$\mu_\mathrm{1D} = \mu_\mathrm{bulk}
\left[1-\left(d/d_0\right)^{-\beta}\right]$. The parameter $d_0$, comparable to
the carrier mean free path, defines a boundary layer exhibiting a considerable
mobility gradient, and also quantifies the competition between e-ph and surface
scattering together with $\beta$. We further discuss the effects of
orientation, cross-sectional shape, and temperature. Moreover, experimental
data are generally lower than our predictions, possibly due to structural
imperfections, systematic errors from measurements, etc. Therefore, our
theoretical method can provide an intrinsic benchmark toward optimized
experimental realizations.

*Hayden Groeschel,Arjyama Bordoloi,Sobhit Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 硫掺杂黑磷（b-P）因其增强的环境稳定性和可调的电子特性而成为下一代电子和光电技术的有前景的候选材料。本研究利用第一性原理密度泛函理论计算，系统研究了硫取代对b-P的弹性、力学和电子特性的影响，并特别关注其负泊松比的特徵。研究结果揭示了b-P内在的负泊松比行为的根本原因，并阐明了硫掺入如何改变这种行为。研究发现，硫原子会扭曲b-P中负责负泊松比的特征性领结结构，从而抑制面内负泊松比。此外，由此产生的电荷重新分布也有效地抑制了b-P的面外负泊松比。随着硫含量的增加，体积模量和泊松比增加，而杨氏模量、剪切模量和德拜温度降低。硫取代还抑制了b-P的半导体特性，导致其呈现金属性。这些发现表明，尽管硫取代增强了b-P的环境稳定性，但它也显著改变了其弹性、力学特性，特别是负泊松比行为，这在设计纳米级电子器件时是一个重要的考量因素。

Result: 硫原子扭曲了b-P的领结结构，抑制了面内负泊松比；电荷重新分布抑制了面外负泊松比；随着硫含量增加，体积模量和泊松比增加，杨氏模量、剪切模量和德拜温度降低；硫取代抑制了b-P的半导体特性，呈现金属性。

Abstract: Sulfur-doped black phosphorus (b-P) has recently emerged as a promising
candidate for next-generation electronic and optoelectronic technologies owing
to its enhanced environmental stability and tunable electronic properties. In
this work, we systematically investigate the effects of sulfur substitution on
the elastic, mechanical, and electronic properties of b-P, with a particular
focus on its auxetic behavior (that is, negative Poisson's ratio), using
first-principles density functional theory calculations. Our results unveil the
fundamental origin of the intrinsic auxetic response in pristine b-P and
elucidate how sulfur incorporation alters this behavior. We find that sulfur
atoms distort the characteristic bow-tie structural motif responsible for the
negative Poisson's ratio in b-P, thereby suppressing the in-plane auxeticity.
Moreover, the resulting charge redistribution also effectively quenches the
out-of-plane auxetic response of b-P. With increasing sulfur content, the bulk
modulus and Poisson's ratio increase, whereas the Young's modulus, shear
modulus, and Debye temperature decrease. Additionally, sulfur substitution
suppresses the semiconducting properties of b-P, giving rise to metallicity.
These findings highlight that although sulfur substitution enhances the
environmental stability of b-P, it also substantially modifies its elastic and
mechanical properties, particularly the auxetic behavior, which is an important
consideration in the design of nanoscale electronic devices.

*Nadine Denis,Akant Sharma,Elena Blundo,Francesca Santangeli,Paolo De Vincenzi,Riccardo Pallucchi,Mitsuki Yukimune,Alexander Vogel,Ilaria Zardo,Antonio Polimeni,Fumitaro Ishikawa,Marta DeLuca*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过氢注入可逆地、可调地、无损地增加 GaAsN 纳米线的带隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过改变化学或结构成分或施加应变来工程化半导体带隙，以优化光子和光电器件的吸收和发射能量。

Method: 通过氢注入增加 GaAsN 纳米线的带隙，随后通过热退火或激光退火进行可逆调谐。

Result: 带隙可增加高达 460 meV，并且光致发光效率可提高一个数量级。通过控制退火条件，带隙移位是可逆的，并且可以连续调谐。

Conclusion: 氢注入为 GaAsN 纳米线提供了可逆、可调的带隙工程，为开发新型量子结构开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Bandgap engineering in semiconductors is required for the development of
photonic and optoelectronic devices with optimized absorption and emission
energies. This is usually achieved by changing the chemical or structural
composition during growth or by dynamically applying strain. Here, the bandgap
in GaAsN nanowires grown on Si is increased post-growth by up to 460 meV in a
reversible, tunable, and non-destructive manner through H implantation. Such a
bandgap tunability is unattained in epilayers and enabled by relaxed strain
requirements in nanowire heterostructures, which enables N concentrations of up
to 4.2% in core-shell GaAs/GaAsN/GaAs nanowires resulting in a GaAsN bandgap as
low as 0.97 eV. Using micro-photoluminescence measurements on individual
nanowires, it is shown that the high bandgap energy of GaAs at 1.42 eV is
restored by hydrogenation through formation of N-H complexes. By carefully
optimizing the hydrogenation conditions, the photoluminescence efficiency
increases by an order of magnitude. Moreover, by controlled thermal annealing,
the large shift of the bandgap is not only made reversible, but also
continuously tuned by breaking up N-H complexes in the hydrogenated GaAsN.
Finally, local bandgap tuning by laser annealing is demonstrated, opening up
new possibilities for developing novel, locally and energy-controlled quantum
structures in GaAsN nanowires.

</details>

### [287] [Optimizing Attention on GPUs by Exploiting GPU Architectural NUMA Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02132)
*Mansi Choudhary,Karthik Sangaiah,Sonali Singh,Muhammad Osama,Lisa Wu Wills,Ganesh Dasika*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: AI GPU 的 disaggregation 暴露出大规模注意力工作负载中的关键瓶颈：NUMA。多芯粒设计已成为扩展计算能力的标准，但内存延迟和带宽在不同计算区域之间差异很大，这会破坏假设统一内存访问的传统 GPU 内核调度策略的性能。我们确定了这些 NUMA 效应对多头注意力 (MHA) 中的局部性造成了怎样的扭曲，并提出了一种空间感知的调度策略 Swizzled Head-first Mapping，该策略将注意力头与 GPU NUMA 域对齐，以利用芯片粒内的缓存重用。在 AMD 的 MI300X 架构上，我们的方法在具有传统调度技术的最新注意力算法上实现了 50% 的更高性能，并保持了 80-97% 的持续高 L2 缓存命中率。这些结果表明，NUMA 感知调度对于在下一代 disaggregated GPU 上实现完全效率至关重要，为可扩展的 AI 训练和推理提供了前进的道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着多芯粒设计成为扩展计算能力的趋势，内存延迟和带宽在不同计算区域之间存在显著差异，这影响了传统的 GPU 内核调度策略，因为它们假设内存访问是统一的。因此，有必要研究 NUMA 效应对大规模注意力工作负载的影响，并开发新的调度策略来解决这些挑战。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Swizzled Head-first Mapping 的空间感知调度策略，该策略将注意力头与 GPU NUMA 域对齐，以利用芯片粒内的缓存重用。

Result: 在 AMD 的 MI300X 架构上，与使用传统调度技术的最新注意力算法相比，该方法实现了高达 50% 的性能提升，并保持了 80-97% 的 L2 缓存命中率。

Conclusion: NUMA 感知调度对于在下一代 disaggregated GPU 上实现最佳效率至关重要，为可扩展的 AI 训练和推理提供了解决方案。

Abstract: The rise of disaggregated AI GPUs has exposed a critical bottleneck in
large-scale attention workloads: non-uniform memory access (NUMA). As
multi-chiplet designs become the norm for scaling compute capabilities, memory
latency and bandwidth vary sharply across compute regions, undermining the
performance of traditional GPU kernel scheduling strategies that assume uniform
memory access. We identify how these NUMA effects distort locality in
multi-head attention (MHA) and present Swizzled Head-first Mapping, a
spatially-aware scheduling strategy that aligns attention heads with GPU NUMA
domains to exploit intra-chiplet cache reuse. On AMD's MI300X architecture, our
method achieves up to 50% higher performance over state-of-the-art attention
algorithms using conventional scheduling techniques and sustains consistently
high L2 cache hit rates of 80-97%. These results demonstrate that NUMA-aware
scheduling is now fundamental to achieving full efficiency on next-generation
disaggregated GPUs, offering a path forward for scalable AI training and
inference.

</details>


### [288] [BoolSkeleton: Boolean Network Skeletonization via Homogeneous Pattern Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02196)
*Liwei Ni,Jiaxi Zhang,Shenggen Zheng,Junfeng Liu,Xingyu Meng,Biwei Xie,Xingquan Li,Huawei Li*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 布尔等价性导致具有相同功能的布尔网络表现出不同的图结构，这既为逻辑优化提供了探索空间，也给涉及布尔网络之间一致性的任务带来了挑战。为应对这一挑战，本文提出了一种新颖的布尔网络骨架化方法BoolSkeleton，以提高设计特定评估的一致性和可靠性。BoolSkeleton包括两个关键步骤：预处理和约简。在预处理中，将布尔网络转换为定义的布尔依赖图，并为节点分配功能相关状态。接下来，为节点级模式约简步骤定义了同质和异质模式。保留异质模式以维持关键功能相关依赖关系，而同质模式则可以约简。模式参数K 进一步约束了这些模式的扇入大小，从而能够对图约简的粒度进行精细控制。为了验证BoolSkeleton的有效性，我们围绕布尔网络进行了压缩分析、分类、关键路径分析和时序预测四个分析/下游任务，证明了其在各种场景下的鲁棒性。此外，与原始布尔网络相比，在时序预测任务上的平均准确率提高了55%以上。这些实验强调了BoolSkeleton在逻辑综合中提高设计一致性的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布尔等价性导致具有相同功能的布尔网络表现出不同的图结构，这既为逻辑优化提供了探索空间，也给涉及布尔网络之间一致性的任务带来了挑战。

Method: BoolSkeleton包括两个关键步骤：预处理和约简。在预处理中，将布尔网络转换为定义的布尔依赖图，并为节点分配功能相关状态。接下来，为节点级模式约简步骤定义了同质和异质模式。保留异质模式以维持关键功能相关依赖关系，而同质模式则可以约简。模式参数K 进一步约束了这些模式的扇入大小，从而能够对图约简的粒度进行精细控制。

Result: 为了验证BoolSkeleton的有效性，我们围绕布尔网络进行了压缩分析、分类、关键路径分析和时序预测四个分析/下游任务，证明了其在各种场景下的鲁棒性。此外，与原始布尔网络相比，在时序预测任务上的平均准确率提高了55%以上。

Conclusion: BoolSkeleton在逻辑综合中具有提高设计一致性的潜力。

Abstract: Boolean equivalence allows Boolean networks with identical functionality to
exhibit diverse graph structures. This gives more room for exploration in logic
optimization, while also posing a challenge for tasks involving consistency
between Boolean networks. To tackle this challenge, we introduce BoolSkeleton,
a novel Boolean network skeletonization method that improves the consistency
and reliability of design-specific evaluations. BoolSkeleton comprises two key
steps: preprocessing and reduction. In preprocessing, the Boolean network is
transformed into a defined Boolean dependency graph, where nodes are assigned
the functionality-related status. Next, the homogeneous and heterogeneous
patterns are defined for the node-level pattern reduction step. Heterogeneous
patterns are preserved to maintain critical functionality-related dependencies,
while homogeneous patterns can be reduced. Parameter K of the pattern further
constrains the fanin size of these patterns, enabling fine-tuned control over
the granularity of graph reduction. To validate BoolSkeleton's effectiveness,
we conducted four analysis/downstream tasks around the Boolean network:
compression analysis, classification, critical path analysis, and timing
prediction, demonstrating its robustness across diverse scenarios. Furthermore,
it improves above 55% in the average accuracy compared to the original Boolean
network for the timing prediction task. These experiments underscore the
potential of BoolSkeleton to enhance design consistency in logic synthesis.

</details>


### [289] [Energy-Efficient Hardware Acceleration of Whisper ASR on a CGLA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02269)
*Takuto Ando,Yu Eto,Ayumu Takeuchi,Yasuhiko Nakashima*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 生成式AI在语音识别（ASR）任务中带来了严峻的能源消耗挑战。ASIC效率高但缺乏可编程性，而通用CGRA（IMAX）则提供了这种灵活性。本研究首次在CGRA上实现了Whisper核心计算内核，并与CPU和GPU进行了性能比较。通过硬件/软件协同设计和FPGA原型，我们预测了28nmASIC的性能，结果显示其能效优于现有方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在ASR任务中能耗高，ASIC效率高但牺牲了可编程性，需要寻找能效和可编程性兼顾的解决方案。

Method: 在IMAX（一种通用粗粒度线性阵列CGRA）上实现并评估了Whisper的核心计算内核，通过FPGA原型进行软硬件协同设计，并预测了28nmASIC的性能。

Result: 在Q8_0模型上，预测的ASIC比NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin能效高1.90倍，比NVIDIA RTX 4090能效高9.83倍。

Conclusion: CGRA平台有潜力成为功耗受限的边缘设备上实现可持续ASR的有前景的平台。

Abstract: The rise of generative AI for tasks like Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR)
has created a critical energy consumption challenge. While ASICs offer high
efficiency, they lack the programmability to adapt to evolving algorithms. To
address this trade-off, we implement and evaluate Whisper's core computational
kernel on the IMAX, a general-purpose Coarse-Grained Linear Arrays (CGLAs)
accelerator. To our knowledge, this is the first work to execute a Whisper
kernel on a CGRA and compare its performance against CPUs and GPUs. Using
hardware/software co-design, we evaluate our system via an FPGA prototype and
project performance for a 28 nm ASIC. Our results demonstrate superior energy
efficiency. The projected ASIC is 1.90x more energy-efficient than the NVIDIA
Jetson AGX Orin and 9.83x more than an NVIDIA RTX 4090 for the Q8_0 model. This
work positions CGLA as a promising platform for sustainable ASR on
power-constrained edge devices.

</details>


### [290] [VFocus: Better Verilog Generation from Large Language Model via Focused Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02285)
*Zhuorui Zhao,Bing Li,Grace Li Zhang,Ulf Schlichtmann*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: VFocus是一个三阶段框架，通过将LLM的推理集中在代码生成过程的关键决策点来增强Verilog代码生成，从而解决了LLM生成Verilog代码的正确性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM生成Verilog代码的方法依赖于自一致性或模拟反馈来选择最佳候选，但未能充分利用LLM的推理能力来关注设计的关键部分，从而影响了生成代码的功能正确性。

Method: VFocus框架包含三个阶段：预排序、排序和后排序优化。预排序阶段生成多个代码候选，进行语法检查，并通过“密度引导过滤”保留在“推理最佳点”内的候选。排序阶段使用自动生成的测试平台模拟每个候选，并通过基于自一致性的聚类来识别最一致的输出。后排序优化阶段对排名靠前的候选进行不一致性挖掘，并调用增强推理的LLM提示进行优化。

Result: 在VerilogEval-Human基准测试上的实验表明，VFocus在多个推理LLM上显著提高了pass@1正确率，证明了其在复杂硬件设计任务中增强Verilog生成方面的有效性。

Conclusion: VFocus通过优化LLM的推理过程，有效解决了LLM在生成Verilog代码时存在的正确性挑战，并在实际测试中取得了显著的改进。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown impressive potential in generating
Verilog codes, but ensuring functional correctness remains a challenge.
Existing approaches often rely on self-consistency or simulation feedback to
select the best candidate, but they miss opportunities to focus LLM reasoning
on the most informative parts of the design. We propose VFocus, a three-stage
framework that enhances Verilog generation by sharpening the focus of LLM
reasoning onto critical decision points in the code generation process. In the
\textbf{pre-ranking stage}, VFocus generates multiple code candidates through
LLM prompting, retries for syntactically valid outputs, and introduces a
\textit{Density-guided Filtering} to retain candidates that fall within the
"reasoning sweet spot" for functional correctness. In the \textbf{ranking
stage}, we simulate each code candidate using an automatically generated
testbench and apply self-consistency-based clustering to identify the most
consistent outputs. Finally, in the \textbf{post-ranking refinement stage},
VFocus performs inconsistency mining on top-ranked candidates and invokes
reasoning-augmented LLM prompts for candidate refinement. Experiments on the
VerilogEval-Human benchmark show that VFocus significantly improves the pass@1
correctness across multiple reasoning LLMs, demonstrating its effectiveness in
enhancing Verilog generation for complex hardware design tasks.

</details>


### [291] [Facial Expression Recognition System Using DNN Accelerator with Multi-threading on FPGA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02408)
*Takuto Ando,Yusuke Inoue*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 通过在 SoC FPGA 上使用 DPU 和多线程技术，实现了高效的多线程人脸表情识别系统，将两个 DNN 推理（人脸检测和表情识别）都部署在 DPU 上，提高了资源利用率和系统吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前的面部表情识别系统在人脸检测阶段使用 CPU 运行 Haar Cascade 检测器，存在准确性问题，并且由于 FPGA 资源限制，无法在 FPGA 上运行第二个 DNN 推理。需要一种更准确、资源利用率更高的方法。

Method: 提出了一种新方法，将人脸检测（使用 DenseBox）和面部表情识别（使用 CNN）都部署在 DPU（一种通用 CNN 加速器）上。并开发了一种多线程技术来提高 DPU 的利用率和系统吞吐量。

Result: 实现了 25 FPS 的整体系统吞吐量，并且功耗效率（吞吐量/功耗）提高了 2.4 倍。

Conclusion: 通过在 SoC FPGA 上集成 DPU 和多线程技术，成功实现了一个高效、资源利用率高的人脸表情识别系统，解决了现有方法的准确性和资源限制问题。

Abstract: In this paper, we implement a stand-alone facial expression recognition
system on an SoC FPGA with multi-threading using a Deep learning Processor Unit
(DPU). The system consists of two steps: one for face detection step and one
for facial expression recognition. In the previous work, the Haar Cascade
detector was run on a CPU in the face detection step due to FPGA resource
limitations, but this detector is less accurate for profile and variable
illumination condition images. Moreover, the previous work used a dedicated
circuit accelerator, so running a second DNN inference for face detection on
the FPGA would require the addition of a new accelerator. As an alternative to
this approach, we run the two inferences by DNN on a DPU, which is a
general-purpose CNN accelerator of the systolic array type. Our method for face
detection using DenseBox and facial expression recognition using CNN on the
same DPU enables the efficient use of FPGA resources while maintaining a small
circuit size. We also developed a multi-threading technique that improves the
overall throughput while increasing the DPU utilization efficiency. With this
approach, we achieved an overall system throughput of 25 FPS and a throughput
per power consumption of 2.4 times.

</details>


### [292] [Digit-Recurrence Posit Division](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02494)
*Raul Murillo,Julio Villalba-Moreno,Alberto A. Del Barrio,Guillermo Botella*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 提出基于查找表方法的posit除法单元，并使用综合评估验证了其在能源效率和面积开销方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Posit算术作为IEEE 754浮点表示的一种有前景的替代方案，提供了更高的精度和动态范围。然而，由于其固有的硬件复杂性，Posit系统中的除法运算仍然具有挑战性。

Method: 在本文中，我们提出了基于查找表和数字递归算法的Posit除法单元，这是在Posit算术背景下首次实现基数-4数字递归技术。我们的方法包含了面向硬件的优化，例如冗余运算、即时商转换和操作数缩放，以简化除法过程，同时减轻延迟、面积和功耗的开销。

Result: 跨多种Posit配置的综合评估表明，与现有方法相比，我们的方法在性能上有了显著的改进，包括能源效率提高80%以上，面积开销却很小，并且迭代次数也大大减少。

Conclusion: 这些结果强调了我们改进后的算法在提高基于Posit的算术单元效率方面的潜力。

Abstract: Posit arithmetic has emerged as a promising alternative to IEEE 754
floating-point representation, offering enhanced accuracy and dynamic range.
However, division operations in posit systems remain challenging due to their
inherent hardware complexity. In this work, we present posit division units
based on the digit-recurrence algorithm, marking the first implementation of
radix-4 digit-recurrence techniques within this context. Our approach
incorporates hardware-centric optimizations including redundant arithmetic,
on-the-fly quotient conversion, and operand scaling to streamline the division
process while mitigating latency, area, and power overheads. Comprehensive
synthesis evaluations across multiple posit configurations demonstrate
significant performance improvements, including more than 80% energy reduction
with small area overhead compared to existing methods, and a substantial
decrease in the number of iterations. These results underscore the potential of
our adapted algorithm to enhance the efficiency of posit-based arithmetic
units.

</details>

Abstract: This paper presents the first implementation and in-depth evaluation of the
primary computational kernels from the stable-diffusion.cpp image generation

project its potential for a future Application-Specific Integrated Circuit
(ASIC) implementation. Our results demonstrate that, despite its
general-purpose architecture, IMAX3 achieves promising performance and power
efficiency, particularly in its projected ASIC form. This work provides
concrete guidelines for future IMAX architectural designs and establishes a
foundation for developing next-generation, AI-specialized Coarse-Grained Linear

multi-modal AI platforms.

### [294] [LGCC: Enhancing Flow Matching Based Text-Guided Image Editing with Local Gaussian Coupling and Context Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01894)
*Fangbing Liu,Pengfei Duan,Wen Li,Yi He*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: LGCC通过局部高斯噪声耦合和内容一致性损失解决了现有图像编辑模型（如BAGEL）在细节丢失、内容不一致和效率低下方面的问题，显著提高了编辑质量和速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于流匹配的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在图像编辑方面存在细节退化、内容不一致和效率低下等问题，主要是由于它们依赖于随机噪声初始化。

Method: 提出了一种名为LGCC的新框架，包含两个关键组件：局部高斯噪声耦合（LGNC）和内容一致性损失（CCL）。LGNC通过将目标图像嵌入及其局部扰动对应物建模为耦合对来保留空间细节，而CCL则确保编辑指令和图像修改之间的语义对齐，防止意外的内容删除。通过课程学习将LGCC与预训练的BAGEL模型集成。

Result: 与BAGEL相比，LGCC在I2EBench上的局部细节分数提高了1.60%，整体分数提高了0.53%。LGCC在轻量级编辑方面实现了3到5倍的速度提升，在通用编辑方面实现了2倍的速度提升，推理时间仅为BAGEL或Flux的40%到50%。

Conclusion: LGCC框架能够有效保留细节、保持上下文完整性并提高推理速度，是一种在不损害编辑质量的前提下提供成本效益的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advancements have demonstrated the great potential of flow
matching-based Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) in image editing.
However, state-of-the-art works like BAGEL face limitations, including detail
degradation, content inconsistency, and inefficiency due to their reliance on
random noise initialization. To address these issues, we propose LGCC, a novel
framework with two key components: Local Gaussian Noise Coupling (LGNC) and
Content Consistency Loss (CCL). LGNC preserves spatial details by modeling
target image embeddings and their locally perturbed counterparts as coupled
pairs, while CCL ensures semantic alignment between edit instructions and image
modifications, preventing unintended content removal. By integrating LGCC with
the BAGEL pre-trained model via curriculum learning, we significantly reduce
inference steps, improving local detail scores on I2EBench by 1.60% and overall
scores by 0.53%. LGCC achieves 3x -- 5x speedup for lightweight editing and 2x
for universal editing, requiring only 40% -- 50% of the inference time of BAGEL
or Flux. These results demonstrate LGCC's ability to preserve detail, maintain
contextual integrity, and enhance inference speed, offering a cost-efficient
solution without compromising editing quality.

</details>

### [295] [EPR Revisited: Context-Indexed Elements of Reality and Operational Completeness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01930)
*Mikołaj Sienicki,Krzysztof Sienicki*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: EPR论证被重新构建，使用操作性方法，并引入了与测量集合相关的上下文索引条件状态，回避了不相容可观测量的值不依赖于上下文的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对EPR论证进行操作性重新构建，并探讨了上下文索引条件状态和操作完备性的概念。

Method: 使用上下文索引条件状态和操作完备性来重新构建EPR论证，并分析了一方无法向另一方发送信号的理论（单方面无信号理论）。

Result: 证明了在单方面无信号理论中，完美的预测允许进行与上下文索引相关的推理，但不能为所有上下文分配固定的值。

Conclusion: 通过分析量子力学可达到的集合的例子（如量子比特单态、连续变量和PR盒的变体），强调了在单方面无信号理论中，虽然可以进行上下文相关的推理，但不能假定存在跨上下文的固定值。

Abstract: We reframe the EPR argument through an operational lens, replacing the notion
of fixed "elements of reality" with context-indexed conditional states - what's
often referred to as a measurement assemblage. This move deliberately sidesteps
the assumption of context-independent values for incompatible observables. Our
updated version of the Reality Criterion works like this: if Alice measures
observable x and obtains outcome a, then Bob's system must adopt a conditional
state that ensures the corresponding outcome for that specific context.
Crucially, we also assume operational completeness - a condition that quantum
mechanics satisfies when we're dealing with quantum-reachable assemblages. Now,
in any theory where one party cannot signal to the other (so-called one-sided
no-signaling theories), perfect predictions do support drawing context-indexed
inferences. But - and this is key - they don't legitimize assigning fixed
values across all contexts. We rigorously demonstrate this distinction. To
ground the argument, we offer examples: the qubit singlet scenario using Pauli
settings and CJWR thresholds, a continuous-variable case based on the Reid
criteria, and a counterexample in the spirit of the PR box, which highlights
the boundaries of what quantum theory can actually reach.

</details>


### [296] [Generation and read-out of many-body Bell correlations with a probe qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01962)
*Marcin Płodzień,Jan Chwedeńczuk*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着量子技术需求的增长，在复杂多体系统中产生和分类非经典关联的需求也日益增加。

Method: 利用单量子比特与 N 量子比特系统相互作用，诱导多体量子关联，并使用单量子比特作为探测器提取关联信息。

Result: 证明了单量子比特与 N 量子比特系统的成对相互作用足以产生多体量子关联，并且单量子比特的测量可以揭示多方纠缠和 N 体贝尔关联。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够快速有效地认证复杂系统中的非经典性。

Abstract: As demand for quantum technologies increases, so does the need to generate
and classify non-classical correlations in complex many-body systems. We
introduce a simple and versatile method for creating and certifying
entanglement and many-body Bell correlations. This method relies on a single
qubit interacting with an $N$-qubit system. We demonstrate that: (i) such
pairwise interaction is sufficient to induce many-body quantum correlations,
and (ii) the qubit can serve as a probe to extract all information about these
correlations. Thus, single-qubit measurements reveal multi-partite entanglement
and $N$-body Bell correlations, enabling the rapid and efficient certification
of non-classicality in complex systems.

### [297] [A Non-Variational Quantum Approach to the Job Shop Scheduling Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26859)
*Miguel Angel Lopez-Ruiz,Emily L. Tucker,Emma M. Arnold,Evgeny Epifanovsky,Ananth Kaushik,Martin Roetteler*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Iterative-QAOA 是一种量子算法变体，旨在克服近期硬件限制，在组合优化问题上取得进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近地面量子硬件的限制阻碍了量子启发式算法在组合优化中的应用。

Method: Iterative-QAOA 采用非变分、浅深度电路方法，并结合了固定参数调度和迭代热启动。

Result: 在 IonQ Forte QPUs 上对 JIT-JSSP 实例进行了基准测试，其性能优于 VarQITE 和 LR-QAOA 算法，并成功收敛到最优或接近最优的解决方案。对更大实例的张量网络模拟表明，该算法具有良好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: Iterative-QAOA 能够有效解决组合优化问题，并有可能在容错量子计算机上解决工业规模的问题。

Abstract: Quantum heuristics offer a potential advantage for combinatorial optimization
but are constrained by near-term hardware limitations. We introduce
Iterative-QAOA, a variant of QAOA designed to mitigate these constraints. The
algorithm combines a non-variational, shallow-depth circuit approach using
fixed-parameter schedules with an iterative warm-starting process. We benchmark
the algorithm on Just-in-Time Job Shop Scheduling Problem (JIT-JSSP) instances
on IonQ Forte Generation QPUs, representing some of the largest such problems
ever executed on quantum hardware. We compare the performance of the algorithm
against both the Variational Quantum Imaginary Time Evolution (VarQITE)
algorithm and the non-variational Linear Ramp (LR) QAOA algorithm. We find that
Iterative-QAOA robustly converges to find optimal solutions as well as
high-quality, near-optimal solutions for all problem instances evaluated. We
evaluate the algorithm on larger problem instances up to 97 qubits using tensor
network simulations. The scaling behavior of the algorithm indicates potential
for solving industrial-scale problems on fault-tolerant quantum computers.

### [298] [Stability of mixed-state phases under weak decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01976)
*Yifan F. Zhang,Sarang Gopalakrishnan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Gibbs 态在弱局部退相干下是稳定的，可以通过局部解码器进行逆转，这表明量子内存和扩散模型中的退相干阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明经典和通勤 Pauli 哈密顿量的 Gibbs 态在弱局部退相干下是稳定的，并且可以局部逆转退相干的影响。

Method: 在存在长程关联和临界减速的系统（包括有限温度平衡临界点和有序低温相）中，推导出局部解码器的存在性。

Result: 证明了存在局部解码器可以撤销退相干效应，只要退相干强度低于某个临界值。

Conclusion: 研究结果意味着热力学稳定的量子内存具有非零的退相干阈值，即使在接近临界温度时也是如此。类似地，在扩散模型中，数据分布的稳定性意味着在后期生成动力学中存在计算上有效的局部去噪器。

Abstract: We prove that the Gibbs states of classical, and commuting-Pauli,
Hamiltonians are stable under weak local decoherence: i.e., we show that the
effect of the decoherence can be locally reversed. In particular, our
conclusions apply to finite-temperature equilibrium critical points and ordered
low-temperature phases. In these systems the unconditional spatio-temporal
correlations are long-range, and local (e.g., Metropolis) dynamics exhibits
critical slowing down. Nevertheless, our results imply the existence of local
"decoders" that undo the decoherence, when the decoherence strength is below a
critical value. An implication of these results is that thermally stable
quantum memories have a threshold against decoherence that remains nonzero as
one approaches the critical temperature. Analogously, in diffusion models,
stability of data distributions implies the existence of
computationally-efficent local denoisers in the late-time generation dynamics.

</details>


### [299] [Entropy-based random quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01988)
*Harry J. D. Miller*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: We construct a new random matrix ensemble for quantum states based on information geometry, finding it has higher purity and can be used for Bayesian quantum state tomography and quantifying entanglement.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to use the natural metric induced by the curvature of von-Neumann entropy and relative entropy in quantum information geometry to construct a new random matrix ensemble for mixed quantum states.

Method: The method involves constructing a random matrix ensemble for quantum states using an information metric derived from the curvature of quantum entropies. This ensemble is generated by sampling a class of bipartite pure states, and its statistical properties, such as eigenvalue density and entropy probability distribution, are investigated. The approach differs from existing Hilbert-Schmidt and Bures-Hall ensembles.

Result: The study finds that the proposed entropy-based random matrix ensemble exhibits a distinguishing feature of larger purity and increased volume towards the boundary of full-rank states compared to existing ensembles.

Conclusion: The entropy-based ensemble serves as a valuable tool for uninformative prior in Bayesian quantum state tomography, particularly in high purity regimes. It can also be utilized for quantifying typical entanglement in finite depth quantum circuits, offering a new perspective and methodology in these areas.

Abstract: In quantum information geometry, the curvature of von-Neumann entropy and
relative entropy induce a natural metric on the space of mixed quantum states.
Here we use this information metric to construct a random matrix ensemble for
states and investigate its key statistical properties such the eigenvalue
density and probability distribution of entropy. We present an algorithm for
generating these entropy-based random density matrices by sampling a class of
bipartite pure states, thus providing a new recipe for random state generation
that differs from the well established Hilbert-Schmidt and Bures-Hall ensemble
approaches. We find that a distinguishing feature of the ensemble is its larger
purity and increased volume towards the boundary of full-rank states. The
entropy-based ensemble can thus be used as a uninformative prior for Bayesian
quantum state tomography in high purity regimes, and as a tool for quantifying
typical entanglement in finite depth quantum circuits.

</details>

identify trade-offs between DV and CV paradigms for quantum-enhanced medical

### [301] [What is special about the Kirkwood-Dirac distributions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01996)
*Matéo Spriet,Christopher Langrenez,Raymond Brummelhuis,Stephan De Bièvre*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Kirkwood-Dirac表征是量子力学中的一种灵活的准概率表征。本文研究了在所有具有正确边际Born概率的准概率表征中，Kirkwood-Dirac表征的独特性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为什么Kirkwood-Dirac表征在所有可能的准概率表征中是特别的？

Method: 研究了在联合谱上定义的、具有正确边际Born概率的准概率表征。证明了对于每个可观测量X，存在一个与之相关的条件期望，给定B。此外，证明了只有Kirkwood-Dirac表征具有其条件期望等于B的函数的最佳预测值的性质。

Result: 对于所有具有正确边际Born概率的准概率表征，都存在一个与每个可观测量X相关的条件期望，给定B。然而，只有Kirkwood-Dirac表征具有其条件期望与B的函数的最佳预测值相匹配的性质。

Conclusion: Kirkwood-Dirac表征因其在所有具有正确边际Born概率的准概率表征中，其条件期望与给定B的X的最佳预测值相匹配而具有独特性。

Abstract: Among all possible quasiprobability representations of quantum mechanics, the
family of Kirkwood-Dirac representations has come to the foreground in recent
years because of the flexibility they offer in numerous applications. This
raises the question of their characterisation: what makes Kirkwood-Dirac
representations special among all possible choices? We show the following. For
two observables $\hat A$ and $\hat B$, consider all quasiprobability
representations of quantum mechanics defined on the joint spectrum of $\hat A$
and $\hat B$, and that have the correct marginal Born probabilities for $\hat
A$ and $\hat B$. For any such Born-compatible quasiprobability representation,
we show that there exists, for each observable $\hat{X}$, a naturally
associated conditional expectation, given $\hat B$. In addition, among the
aforementioned representations, only the Kirkwood-Dirac representation has the
following property: its associated conditional expectation of $\hat{X}$ given
$\hat{B}$ coincides with the best predictor of $\hat{X}$ by a function of $\hat
B$, for all $\hat X$.

</details>


### [302] [Spread and circuit complexity as a measure of particle content and phase space fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02013)
*Satyaki Chowdhury*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本工作研究了量子复杂度（电路复杂度、扩展复杂度）与粒子含量、位置和动量算符方差等物理量之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子复杂度与粒子含量、位置和动量算符方差等物理量之间的关系，为量子场论在弯曲背景下的研究提供新的见解。

Method: 使用具有时变质量和频率的谐振子作为玩具模型，分析电路复杂度和扩展复杂度与平均量子数及其变化率、位置和动量算符方差的关系。

Result: 电路复杂度和扩展复杂度由平均量子数及其变化率决定，并与位置和动量算符的方差直接相关。

Conclusion: 量子复杂度可以被清晰地解释为量子态的激发和相空间涨落，并且在时变振荡器模型中，扩展复杂度和电路复杂度之间存在精确且普遍的关系。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the relation between different notions of
quantum complexity, namely, circuit and spread complexity and physically
meaningful quantities such as the particle content of the quantum state and the
variances of position and momentum operators. Using a harmonic oscillator with
time-dependent mass and frequency as a toy model, we show that both circuit and
spread complexity at any instant is determined by the mean number of quanta and
its rate of change. Furthermore, both complexity and its growth are directly
linked to the variances of the position and momentum operators, providing a
clear physical interpretation of complexity in terms of the state's excitation
and phase-space fluctuation. Although the analysis is carried out for a single
time-dependent oscillator, the results have direct relevance for quantum field
theory in curved backgrounds, where individual field modes effectively behave
as time-dependent oscillators. This offers new insights into how quantum
complexity encodes particle production and phase space fluctuations in
non-holographic systems. Finally, we establish a precise and potentially
universal relation between spread and circuit complexity for the time evolved
state suggesting deeper connections between different complexity measures in
the context of field theories on curved backgrounds.

</details>

fluorescent label for biomolecules.

### [304] [Efficient Variational Quantum Algorithms for the Generalized Assignment Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02739)
*Carlo Mastroianni,Francesco Plastina,Jacopo Settino,Andrea Vinci*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: VQGAP是一种用于解决广义分配问题(GAP)的混合量子-经典算法，它通过优化量子资源和减少所需参数化量子电路宽度来提高效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: VQGAP通过引入编码/解码函数，将量子线路生成的解映射到问题变量空间，从而解耦了量子线路的qubits和GAP的二元变量，并利用问题约束来优化量子资源。

Abstract: Quantum algorithms offer a compelling new avenue for addressing difficult
NP-complete optimization problems, such as the Generalized Assignment Problem
(GAP). Given the operational constraints of contemporary Noisy
Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) devices, hybrid quantum-classical approaches,
specifically Variational Quantum Algorithms (VQAs) like the Variational Quantum
Eigensolver (VQE), promises to be effective approaches to solve real-world
optimization problems. This paper proposes an approach, named VQGAP, designed
to efficiently solve the GAP by optimizing quantum resources and reducing the
required parametrized quantum circuit width with respect to standard VQE. The
main idea driving our proposal is to decouple the qubits of ansatz circuits
from the binary variables of the General Assignment Problem, by providing
encoding/decoding functions transforming the solutions generated by ansatze in
the limited quantum space in feasible solutions in the problem variables space,
by exploiting the constraints of the problem. Preliminary results, obtained
through both noiseless and noisy simulations, indicate that VQGAP exhibits
performance and behavior very similar to VQE, while effectively reducing the
number of qubits and circuit depth.

### [307] [ZZ-Free Two-Transmon CZ Gate Mediated by a Fluxonium Coupler](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02115)
*Junyoung An,Helin Zhang,Qi Ding,Leon Ding,Youngkyu Sung,Roni Winik,Junghyun Kim,Ilan T. Rosen,Kate Azar,Renee DePencier Piñero,Jeffrey M. Gertler,Michael Gingras,Bethany M. Method: 提出TFT（Transmon-Fluxonium-Transmon）架构，其中两个跨度量子比特通过一个通量量子比特进行耦合。利用通量量子比特作为耦合介质，即使在量子比特-量子比特失谐大于其非简谐性的情况下，也能消除残余ZZ相互作用。通过实验识别了两个不同的TFT设备中量子比特-量子比特失谐分别为409MHz和616MHz的零ZZ相互作用点。随后，在两个设备上实现了绝热的、由耦合器磁通偏置控制的受控Z门。

Abstract: Eliminating residual ZZ interactions in a two-qubit system is essential for
reducing coherent errors during quantum operations. In a superconducting
circuit platform, coupling two transmon qubits via a transmon coupler has been
shown to effectively suppress residual ZZ interactions. However, in such
systems, perfect cancellation usually requires the qubit-qubit detuning to be
smaller than the individual qubit anharmonicities, which exacerbates frequency
crowding and microwave crosstalk. To address this limitation, we introduce TFT
(Transmon-Fluxonium-Transmon) architecture, wherein two transmon qubits are
coupled via a fluxonium qubit. The coupling mediated by the fluxonium
eliminates residual ZZ interactions even for transmons detuned larger than
their anharmonicities. We experimentally identified zero-ZZ interaction points
at qubit-qubit detunings of 409 MHz and 616 MHz from two distinct TFT devices.
We then implemented an adiabatic, coupler-flux-biased controlled-Z gate on both
devices, achieving CZ gate fidelities of 99.64(6)% and 99.68(8)%.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 创建可扩展、可靠且经过充分论证的量子计算机基准测试具有挑战性，因为简单的方法存在指数级扩展、对重要错误不敏感或使用未经充分论证的性能指标等问题。此外，精心策划的基准测试套件无法包含所有有趣的量子电路或算法，因此需要一个能够轻松创建新基准测试的工具。

Method: 该软件采用高效的保真度估算技术，包括镜像电路保真度估算和子电路体积基准测试，以创建高效且可靠的基准测试。它提供了一个简单的接口，使得非量子计算机基准测试或噪声理论方面的专家用户也能创建可靠的基准测试。

Result: ‘scarab’能够创建可扩展且可靠的基准测试，这些基准测试可以测量用户选择的量子电路和算法的充分论证的性能指标（过程保真度）。它能够处理包含数千甚至数百万个量子比特的电路。通过使用‘scarab’，研究人员能够将现有的低效基准测试转换为高效基准测试，创建用于探究哈密顿量模拟中的硬件和算法权衡的基准测试，量化近似电路编译的原位功效，并创建使用子电路来衡量执行感兴趣电路进展情况的基准测试。

Conclusion: ‘scarab’是一个强大的软件工具，可以创建可扩展、可靠且经过充分论证的量子计算机基准测试，并且易于使用，即使对于非专业用户也是如此。它通过采用高效的保真度估算技术，解决了现有基准测试方法的局限性，并为各种应用提供了灵活性。

Abstract: Creating scalable, reliable, and well-motivated benchmarks for quantum
computers is challenging: straightforward approaches to benchmarking suffer
from exponential scaling, are insensitive to important errors, or use
poorly-motivated performance metrics. Furthermore, curated benchmarking suites
cannot include every interesting quantum circuit or algorithm, which
necessitates a tool that enables the easy creation of new benchmarks. In this
work, we introduce a software tool for creating scalable and reliable
benchmarks that measure a well-motivated performance metric (process fidelity)
from user-chosen quantum circuits and algorithms. Our software, called
$\texttt{scarab}$, enables the creation of efficient and robust benchmarks even
from circuits containing thousands or millions of qubits, by employing
efficient fidelity estimation techniques, including mirror circuit fidelity
estimation and subcircuit volumetric benchmarking. $\texttt{scarab}$ provides a
simple interface that enables the creation of reliable benchmarks by users who
are not experts in the theory of quantum computer benchmarking or noise. We
demonstrate the flexibility and power of $\texttt{scarab}$ by using it to turn
existing inefficient benchmarks into efficient benchmarks, to create benchmarks
that interrogate hardware and algorithmic trade-offs in Hamiltonian simulation,
to quantify the in-situ efficacy of approximate circuit compilation, and to
create benchmarks that use subcircuits to measure progress towards executing a
circuit of interest.

### [310] [Preserving fermionic statistics for single-particle approximations in microscopic quantum master equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02160)

Method: 提出一个系统-环境参数的数学约束，以确保微观推导的马尔可夫主方程在应用于约化系统时能保持费米子和N-可表统计。在统一主方程、通用Lindblad方程和Redfield主方程中验证了该约束，并探讨了添加泡利因子以恢复N-可表性的方法。

Abstract: Microscopic master equations have gained traction for the dissipative
treatment of molecular spin and solid-state systems for quantum technologies.
Single particle approximations are often invoked to treat these systems, which
can lead to unphysical evolution when combined with master equation approaches.
We present a mathematical constraint on the system-environment parameters to
ensure that microscopically-derived Markovian master equations preserve
fermionic, $N$-representable statistics when applied to reduced systems. We
demonstrate these constraints for the recently derived unified master equation
and universal Lindblad equation, along with the Redfield master equation for
cases when positivity issues are not present. For operators that break the
constraint, we explore the addition of Pauli factors to recover
$N$-representability. This work promotes feasible applications of novel
microscopic master equations for realistic chemical systems.

### [311] [Information recycling in coherent state discrimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02163)
*L. F. Melo,János A. Bergou,Alexandre B. Tacla*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 利用信息回收策略，在区分N个相位对称相干态方面，取得了一定的进展，该策略结合了确定性区分和最小错误区分的优点，在降低误码率的同时，也能提供确定性的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子通信和量子密钥分发（CV-QKD）中，区分相干态是至关重要的，本研究旨在提出并分析一种区分N个相位对称相干态的策略。

Method: 提出了一种信息回收（IR）策略，该策略将最优无歧视区分（UD）的“失败”状态进行再利用，通过顺序最小错误区分（MED）来进一步区分，以期在区分相干态时获得确定性结果，同时允许一部分结果无误。

Result: 研究表明，对于N>2，UD的“失败”状态保留了关于原始输入状态的残余信息，这些信息可以通过顺序MED被最优地回收。信息回收（IR）策略结合了MED和UD的优点，能够提供确定性的结果，并且一部分结果是无差错的。infidelity是衡量状态分离图造成的干扰的指标，它约束了回收阶段的错误概率。在低振幅区域，状态分离在区分时成功率高，对输入状态的干扰小。

Conclusion: 信息回收（IR）策略为连续变量设置中的自适应和顺序区分协议开辟了新的可能性，并可能用于设计下一代量子通信接收器。

Abstract: The discrimination of coherent states is a crucial component in quantum
communication with continuous variables, especially in quantum key distribution
protocols (CV-QKD), which rely on the ability to distinguish among different
coherent states to establish a shared secret key between two parties. Here, we
propose and analyze a strategy for distinguishing among N phase-symmetric
coherent states, which optimally takes unambiguous discrimination (UD) to the
deterministic regime, at the inevitable cost of having non-zero probability of
error. Despite the disturbance introduced by the separation map used in the UD
process, we show that for N > 2, the "failure" states of UD retain residual
information about the original input states, which can be further used for
discrimination. Rather than discarding inconclusive outcomes as in conventional
UD, we show that the "failure" states of UD can be optimally recycled by
performing a sequential minimum-error discrimination (MED). This strategy,
which we call information recycling (IR), combines the benefits of both MED and
optimal UD: It always provides conclusive results while allowing for a subset
of those results to be error-free, which are identifiable by an ancillary
system. We characterize the disturbance introduced by the state separation map
by the infidelity between input and failure states, demonstrating that it lower
bounds the error probability in the recycling stage. Furthermore, in the
low-amplitude regime-relevant for long-distance CV-QKD applications-we show
that the state separation achieves significant success while introducing
relatively low disturbance to the input states after failed events. Our results
open up new possibilities for adaptive and sequential discrimination protocols
in continuous-variable settings, and could potentially be used in the design of
next-generation receivers in quantum communication.

Abstract: Precise control of superconducting qubits is essential for advancing both
quantum simulation and quantum error correction. Recently, transmon qubit
systems employing the single-transmon coupler (STC) scheme have demonstrated
high-fidelity single- and two-qubit gate operations by dynamically tuning the
effective coupling between qubits. However, the integration of STCs increases

line multiplexing scheme based on a double-transmon coupler (DTC) architecture,

iSWAP gate. To validate the practical applicability of this multiplexing

multiplexed DTC architecture offers significant potential to minimize wiring
overhead in two-dimensional qubit arrays, thereby greatly enhancing the
scalability of superconducting quantum processors.

correlations in bright structured twin beams generated via a four-wave mixing
process in a double-$\Lambda$ configuration in atomic vapor. We derive an
analytical expression describing the evolution of the spatial quantum
correlation distribution from the near field to the far field. To qualitatively
support the theoretical predictions, we perform experiments measuring
intensity-difference noise between different spatial subregions of the twin
beams as they propagate from the near field to the far field. The presence of
quantum correlations is manifested as squeezing in the intensity difference
noise measurement. With a Gaussian pump, we observe localized correlations in
the near field and localized anti-correlations in the far field. In contrast,
with a structured Laguerre-Gaussian pump, there is a transition from localized
correlations in the near field to delocalized correlations in the far field.
The present results offer valuable insights into the fundamental behavior of
spatial quantum correlations and open possibilities for potential applications
in quantum information, quantum imaging and sensing.

</details>

### [316] [Dirac delta-convergence of free-motion time-of-arrival eigenfunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02307)
*John Jaykel P. Magadan,Eric A. Galapon*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Previous numerical analyses on the Aharonov-Bohm (AB) operator representing

indicated that its eigenfunctions represent quantum states with definite

proof that this is indeed the case. An essential element of this proof is the
consideration of the eigenfunctions of the AB operator with complex
eigenvalues. These eigenfunctions can be considered legitimate TOA

time equal to the real part of the eigenvalue forms a dirac delta sequence in
the limit as the imaginary part of the eigenvalue approaches zero.

### [321] [Secure PAC Learning: Sample-Budget Laws and Quantum Data-Path Admissibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02479)
*Jeongho Bang*

Main category: quant-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个基于PAC理论的安全学习理论，并构建了一个操作框架，将数据通路行为与有限样本预算联系起来。该框架使用基于运行的序贯检验来评估准确性-置信度目标，并为数据通路通道的可接受性提供了一个封闭形式的预算边界。在量子信息背景下，将数据通路可接受性设置为由Holevo信息确定的阈值，而不是学习者可调的容差。

Result: 开发了一个理论框架，将安全性与PAC学习中的操作样本预算定律相结合，并将安全性锚定在量子信息中。在准备-测量场景下，实现了量子安全PAC学习，其中学习者的信息优势直接转化为学习安全性，这是经典情况所没有的。

Conclusion: 该框架是第一个同时在PAC学习中嵌入安全概念和操作样本预算定律，并将安全性锚定在量子信息中的完整框架。其蓝图为学习安全性提供了标准化保证，并为PAC-Bayes扩展和与先进的量子机器学习前端集成提供了明确的途径。

Abstract: Security in machine learning is fragile when data are exfiltrated or
perturbed, yet existing frameworks rarely connect the definition and analysis
of the security to learnability. In this work, we develop a theory of secure
learning grounded in the probably-approximately-correct (PAC) viewpoint and
develop an operational framework that links data-path behavior to finite-sample
budgets. In our formulation, an accuracy-confidence target is evaluated via a
run-based sequential test that halts after a prescribed number of consecutive
validations, and a closed-form budget bound guarantees the learning success if
the data-path channel is admissible; the acceptance must also exceed a
primitive random-search baseline. We elevate and complete our secure-learning
construction in the context of quantum information -- establishing
quantum-secure PAC learning: for prepare-and-measure scenarios, the data-path
admissibility is set to be threshold fixed by Holevo information, not a
learner-tunable tolerance. Thus, a certified information advantage for the
learner directly becomes the learning security -- an effect with no classical
analogue. The channel-determined confidence follows naturally and basis sifting
is incorporated for practical deployments. This is the first complete framework
that simultaneously embeds a security notion and an operational sample-budget
law within the PAC learning and anchors the security in quantum information.
The resulting blueprint points toward standardized guarantees for the learning
security, with clear avenues for PAC-Bayes extensions and for integration with
advanced quantum machine learning front ends.

Method: 我们实现了一个光量子处理器，其中包含一个变分量子自编码器，它利用光子的路径、偏振和时序模式来学习数据的隐藏对称性（例如 $\mathbb{Z}_2 	imes \mathbb{Z}_2$ 或 $\mathbb{Z}_4$）。该编码器使用梯度下降进行训练，并尝试了两种电路结构：参数化傅里叶变换和用于 Simon 对称问题的通用结构。

Abstract: We experimentally demonstrate quantum data compression exploiting hidden
subgroup symmetries using a photonic quantum processor. Classical databases
containing generalized periodicities-symmetries that are in the worst cases
inefficient for known classical algorithms to be detect-can efficiently
compressed by quantum hidden subgroup algorithms. We implement a variational
quantum autoencoder that autonomously learns both the symmetry type (e.g.,
$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ vs. $\mathbb{Z}_4$) and the generalized
period from structured data. The system uses single photons encoded in path,
polarization, and time-bin degrees of freedom, with electronically controlled
waveplates enabling tunable quantum gates. Training via gradient descent
successfully identifies the hidden symmetry structure, achieving compression by
eliminating redundant database entries. We demonstrate two circuit ansatzes: a
parametrized generalized Fourier transform and a less-restricted architecture
for Simon's symmetry. Both converge successfully, with the cost function
approaching zero as training proceeds. These results provide experimental
proof-of-principle that photonic quantum computers can compress classical
databases by learning symmetries inaccessible to known efficient classical
methods, opening pathways for quantum-enhanced information processing.

TL;DR: This paper presents advances in long-distance quantum key distribution (QKD) for quantum internet networks, demonstrating continuous operation over 325 hours on a 50km link and extending secure key distribution to a 100km link compatible with satellite connections. It also showcases QKD using wavelength demultiplexing across multiple ITU channels via the BBM92 protocol and time-energy observables.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Quantum links are crucial for quantum internet and secure communication, but practical challenges like time synchronisation, interferometer stabilisation, and automation need to be addressed for long-distance QKD.

Method: The paper demonstrates several advances: 1. Continuous operation of an QKD link for 325 hours over 50km. 2. Extension of secure key distribution to a 100km link. 3. Use of wavelength demultiplexing to perform QKD across multiple ITU channels using the BBM92 protocol and time-energy observables.

Result: A 50km QKD link was operated continuously for 325 hours. Secure key distribution was achieved over a 100km link. QKD was successfully performed across multiple ITU channels using the BBM92 protocol and time-energy observables.

Conclusion: The reported advances demonstrate the feasibility of long-duration, long-distance QKD, paving the way for practical quantum internet networks and quantum satellite communication.

Abstract: Entanglement-based quantum links are the backbone of future quantum internet
networks, enabling secure communication between distant cities. Realizing such
networks requires addressing multiple practical challenges in long-distance
quantum key distribution : time synchronisation, interferometer stabilisation
and automation. Here, we report several advances. First, we maintained an
operational QKD link continuously for 325hours over 50km between two remotes
locations, demonstrating the feasibility of long-duration key generation. We
further extended secure key distribution up to a 100km operational link
connecting the University of Nice to a ground-based optical station, a setup
compatible with future quantum satellite connections. Finally, by employing
wavelength demultiplexing to separate photons of entangled pairs, we performed
QKD across multiple ITU channels, achieving secure key exchange via the BBM92
protocol and time-energy observables.

</details>


### [327] [Collective Quantum Batteries and Charger-Battery Setup in Open Quantum Systems: Impact of Inter-Qubit Interactions, Dissipation, and Quantum Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02583)
*Mahima Yadav,Devvrat Tiwari,Subhashish Banerjee*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了两种量子比特开放系统模型在量子电池方面的应用，并研究了相互作用、环境影响以及量子临界性对量子电池性能的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子电池在能量存储和传输方面的潜力，并探索影响其性能的因素。

Method: 研究了三种两比特开放量子系统模型：1. 包含中心自旋和自旋浴的模型，研究了比特间相互作用的影响。2. 与压缩热浴相互作用的模型，研究了原子间距离和浴温度的影响。3. 由充电器和电池组成的模型，其中充电器与各向异性自旋链浴相互作用，并研究了量子临界性的影响。

Result: 展示了量子比特间的相互作用、与环境（如自旋浴、压缩热浴、各向异性自旋链浴）的相互作用以及量子临界性对量子电池的能量存储和传输性能有显著影响。

Conclusion: 量子电池的性能受到多种因素的影响，包括量子比特间的相互作用、与环境的耦合方式以及量子临界性等，这些因素为优化量子电池的设计提供了方向。

Abstract: Quantum batteries have emerged as promising platforms for exploring energy
storage and transfer processes governed by quantum mechanical laws. In this
work, we study three models of two-qubit open quantum systems. The first model
comprises two central spins immersed in spin baths, and both central spins are
collectively considered as quantum batteries. The impact of inter-qubit
interactions on the performance of the quantum battery is investigated. In the
second model, a two-qubit model interacting with a squeezed thermal bath serves
as a collective quantum battery, where the impact of inter-atomic distance and
the bath temperature on the battery's performance is explored. Furthermore, a
two-qubit model is used, where one qubit is modeled as a battery and the other
as a charger. The charger in this model interacts with an anisotropic
spin-chain bath, which is conducive to quantum criticality. It is demonstrated
that this criticality has a substantial impact on the quantum battery's storage
capacity.

### [328] [Trustworthy Quantum Machine Learning: A Roadmap for Reliability, Robustness, and Security in the NISQ Era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02602)
*Ferhat Ozgur Catak,Jungwon Seo,Umit Cali*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子机器学习（QML）在解决经典人工智能难以应对的计算问题方面具有巨大潜力。然而，量子力学的内在概率性、NISQ硬件的设备噪声以及混合量子-经典执行流程带来了新的风险，阻碍了QML在现实世界、安全关键设置中的可靠部署。

Method: 研究中，我们形式化了基于量子信息论的量子特定信任度量，包括：基于方差的预测不确定性分解、迹距离有界鲁棒性以及混合学习信道的差分隐私。为了在当前的NISQ设备上验证其可行性，我们在参数化量子分类器上验证了一个统一的信任度评估流程。

Result: 该评估揭示了不确定性与预测风险之间的相关性、经典和量子态扰动之间攻击脆弱性的不对称性，以及由量子比特数噪声和量子信道噪声驱动的隐私-效用权衡。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的TQML路线图旨在将可信赖性作为量子AI的首要设计目标，通过整合不确定性量化、对抗鲁棒性和隐私保护，为实现可靠的量子机器学习提供了方向。

Abstract: Quantum machine learning (QML) is a promising paradigm for tackling
computational problems that challenge classical AI. Yet, the inherent
probabilistic behavior of quantum mechanics, device noise in NISQ hardware, and
hybrid quantum-classical execution pipelines introduce new risks that prevent
reliable deployment of QML in real-world, safety-critical settings. This
research offers a broad roadmap for Trustworthy Quantum Machine Learning
(TQML), integrating three foundational pillars of reliability: (i) uncertainty
quantification for calibrated and risk-aware decision making, (ii) adversarial
robustness against classical and quantum-native threat models, and (iii)
privacy preservation in distributed and delegated quantum learning scenarios.
We formalize quantum-specific trust metrics grounded in quantum information
theory, including a variance-based decomposition of predictive uncertainty,
trace-distance-bounded robustness, and differential privacy for hybrid learning
channels. To demonstrate feasibility on current NISQ devices, we validate a
unified trust assessment pipeline on parameterized quantum classifiers,
uncovering correlations between uncertainty and prediction risk, an asymmetry
in attack vulnerability between classical and quantum state perturbations, and
privacy-utility trade-offs driven by shot noise and quantum channel noise. This
roadmap seeks to define trustworthiness as a first-class design objective for
quantum AI.

### [329] [Adaptive Quantum Matter: Variational Organization through Ising Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02636)
*Lakshya Nagpal,Syed. R. Hassan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出了自适应量子伊辛代理（AQIA）框架，该框架基于哈密顿量，将可编程量子物质扩展到自适应领域。代理作为有限的横向场伊辛子系统运行，通过依赖状态的反馈通道进行交互，这些通道由自旋极化、键相关和内部能量等简化可观测量表征。这些信息耦合能够将静态晶格转化为可反馈重构的介质。迭代生成的有效哈密顿量通过平均场近似进行自洽求解，其中反馈场被迭代调整以最小化总能量。数值研究确定了三个不同的区域：反馈-涨落临界点附近的畴形成、竞争反馈通道导致的类玻璃挫折，以及由结构化相互作用维持的模块化极化。这些现象独立于几何嵌入发生，表明仅信息相似性就可诱导相干组织。AQIA框架可适用于超导、离子阱或里德堡平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自适应量子伊辛代理（AQIA）框架的提出，旨在将可编程量子物质扩展到自适应领域，探索信息耦合在组织量子系统中的作用。

Method: AQIA框架使用哈密顿量作为基础，每个代理是一个有限的横向场伊辛子系统。代理通过包含自旋极化、键相关和内部能量等简化可观测量的信息反馈通道进行交互。通过平均场近似和迭代调整反馈场来最小化总能量，以自洽地求解生成的有效哈密顿量。

Result: 数值研究发现了三个独特的现象：1. 在反馈-涨落临界点附近出现畴的形成。2. 由于存在竞争的反馈通道，表现出类玻璃挫折。3. 通过结构化的相互作用维持模块化极化。这些现象的发生不依赖于具体的几何结构，表明信息上的相似性足以驱动相干组织。

Conclusion: AQIA框架提供了一个最小化的模型，可用于探索自组织和学习在自适应可编程量子物质中的应用，并且该框架能够适应超导、离子阱或里德堡等多种量子计算平台。

Abstract: The study introduces the Adaptive Quantum Ising Agents (AQIA) framework, a
Hamiltonian-based methodology that extends programmable quantum matter into an
adaptive domain. Each agent operates as a finite transverse-field Ising
subsystem, maintaining internal quantum coherence while interacting through
state-dependent feedback channels characterised by reduced observables such as
spin polarisation, bond correlation, and internal energy. These informational
couplings enable the transformation of a static lattice into a
feedback-reconfigurable medium. The effective Hamiltonian generated, which
remains Hermitian at each iteration, is resolved self-consistently using a
mean-field approximation, where the feedback fields are iteratively adjusted to
minimise the total energy. Numerical investigations identify three distinct
regimes: domain formation near the feedback--fluctuation critical point,
glass-like frustration due to competing feedback channels, and modular
polarisation sustained by structured interactions. These phenomena occur
independently of geometric embedding, illustrating that informational
similarity alone can induce coherent organisation. The AQIA framework is
adaptable to implementation on superconducting, trapped-ion, or Rydberg
platforms, offering a minimalistic model for exploring self-organisation and
learning in adaptive programmable quantum matter.

</details>


### [330] [Resource-efficient variational quantum solver for the travelling salesman problem and its silicon photonics implementation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02696)
*Alessio Baldazzi,Stefano Azzini,Lorenzo Pavesi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种新颖的变分量子算法来解决旅行商问题，使用纠缠量子寄存器来编码城市间的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旅行商问题是经典机器的计算难题。

Method: 制备两个最大纠缠的量子寄存器，其相关性被分配给城市对之间的不同路径。对于 N 个城市，需要 2 ⌈log_2 N⌉ 个量子比特，并且问题的解决方案直接在构成总体试探态的两个寄存器的相关矩阵中找到。

Result: 作为概念验证实验，我们在具有集成光子对源的可重构室温硅光子电路上为具有四个城市的通用问题实现了该算法。

Conclusion: 通过纠缠量子寄存器和相关矩阵来解决旅行商问题，并在光子电路上进行了实验验证。

Abstract: The travelling salesman problem is a well-known example of
computationally-hard combinatorial problem for classical machines. Here, we
propose a novel variational quantum algorithm to solve it. The method is based
on the preparation of two maximally entangled quantum registers whose
correlations are assigned to different paths between pairs of cities. For $N$
cities, this encoding requires $2 \lceil\log_2 N\rceil$ qubits and the solution
to the problem is directly found in the correlation matrix of the two registers
composing the overall trial state. As a proof-of-concept experiment, we
implement this algorithm for generic problems with four cities on a
reconfigurable room-temperature silicon photonic circuit with integrated
photon-pair sources, used to initialize maximally entangled path-encoded
single-photon states.

</details>

Abstract: Quantum emitters coupled to nanophotonic structures are an excellent platform

review brings together key theoretical techniques from quantum optics, their
applications to controllable single-photon transport, and the experimental
realization of single-photon switching devices across different physical
platforms, including semiconductor quantum dots, neutral atoms, superconducting
qubits, and color centers.

Abstract: We find a process satisfying the axioms of hyper-decoherence which produces

opposing conclusions: that the existence of this map might be evidence of a
genuine hyper-decoherence process producing causal quantum theory from its
causally-indefinite higher-order theory; or that it serves as an indication
that the axioms of hyper-decoherence might need careful re-consideration,
especially regarding the subtle albeit central role that purity plays.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用密度矩阵形式和耦合麦克斯韦-布洛赫方程推导了探针和生成光束的解析表达式，其中明确包含铒离子浓度。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate coherent orbital-angular-momentum (OAM) transfer
and dispersion-controlled light propagation in a ladder-type Er YAG three-level
system. Using the density-matrix formalism and coupled Maxwell-Bloch equations,
we derive analytical expressions for the probe and generated beams that
explicitly incorporate Er ion concentration. We show that an incident
vortex-carrying probe beam transfers its OAM to a generated signal beam through
a concentration-dependent sum-frequency nonlinear process, with complete phase
and topological-charge preservation. By analyzing conversion efficiency,
spatial phase, and intensity distributions, we identify an optimal Er
concentration (3 percent) that maximizes vortex-transfer efficiency.
Furthermore, the absorption and dispersion spectra of the probe and generated
beams reveal the mechanism underpinning the vortex transfer and demonstrate
tunable transitions between fast and slow regimes. These results establish Er
YAG as a viable solid-state platform for the coherent manipulation of
structured light, enabling efficient vortex-beam frequency conversion and
dispersion engineering for applications in high-dimensional quantum
communication, wavelength-compatible OAM interfaces, and slow-light photonic
signal processing.

### [334] [On the origin of exponential operator growth in Hilbert space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.02800)
*Vijay Ganesh Sadhasivam,Jan M. Rost,Stuart C. Althorpe*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Krylov复杂性分析表明，算子矩阵元的离对角线衰减可以预测希尔伯特空间中算子的指数增长。非混沌系统可以产生指数增长甚至最大增长，而混沌系统可以表现出亚指数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Krylov复杂性在简单模型中的增长，并将其与算子矩阵元的离对角线衰减联系起来，以预测希尔伯特空间中算子的增长。

Method: 通过分析简单模型中Krylov复杂性的增长，并研究算子矩阵元的离对角线衰减。

Result: 发现算子矩阵元的离对角线衰减（指数或更慢）与Krylov复杂性的指数增长相关；代数衰减或更慢与最大增长率相关。非混沌系统可以产生指数或最大增长，混沌系统可以表现出亚指数增长。

Conclusion: Krylov复杂性的增长模式（指数或最大）取决于算子矩阵元的离对角线衰减模式，并且可以由非混沌和混沌系统产生。

Abstract: By analysing the growth of Krylov complexity for some simple models, we find
that the exponential growth of an operator in Hilbert space can be predicted
from the off-diagonal decay of the operator matrix elements in the system
eigenbasis. When the decay is exponential or slower, the Krylov complexity
grows exponentially; when it is algebraic or slower, the growth rate is
maximal. As a result, non-chaotic systems can generate exponential or even
maximal operator growth, and chaotic systems can show sub-exponential growth;
we give examples of both.

</details>

### [335] [DiffPace: Diffusion-based Plug-and-play Augmented Channel Estimation in mmWave and Terahertz Ultra-Massive MIMO Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.01867)
*Zhengdong Hu,Chong Han,Wolfgang Gerstacker,Robert Schober*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: DiffPace是一种基于扩散模型的即插即用方法，用于毫米波和太赫兹超大规模MIMO系统中的信道估计，提高了精度和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了满足下一代无线网络不断增长的数据速率需求，毫米波和太赫兹通信提供了巨大的带宽，但需要超大规模MIMO和混合波束形成来克服高频固有的路径损耗和降低硬件成本。然而，高信道维度、有限的射频链观测以及混合近场和远场辐射模式给信道估计带来了挑战。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为DiffPace的基于扩散模型的即插即用方法。该方法利用扩散模型（DM）学习混合球形和平面波模型（HPSM）下的信道分布，并将DM作为先验知识来提高信道估计精度。DM通过求解常微分方程进行推理，减少了推理步数。

Result: 实验结果表明，DiffPace在10 dB信噪比下达到了-15 dB的归一化均方误差（NMSE），与现有技术相比，推理步数减少了90%，实现了高估计精度和计算效率。

Conclusion: DiffPace通过利用扩散模型作为先验知识，克服了传统压缩感知方法在处理混合近远场信道结构时的局限性，在精度和效率方面均表现优于现有技术。

Abstract: Millimeter-wave (mmWave) and Terahertz (THz)-band communications hold great
promise in meeting the growing data-rate demands of next-generation wireless
networks, offering abundant bandwidth. To mitigate the severe path loss
inherent to these high frequencies and reduce hardware costs, ultra-massive
multiple-input multiple-output (UM-MIMO) systems with hybrid beamforming
architectures can deliver substantial beamforming gains and enhanced spectral
efficiency. However, accurate channel estimation (CE) in mmWave and THz UM-MIMO
systems is challenging due to high channel dimensionality and compressed
observations from a limited number of RF chains, while the hybrid near- and
far-field radiation patterns, arising from large array apertures and high
carrier frequencies, further complicate CE. Conventional compressive sensing
based frameworks rely on predefined sparsifying matrices, which cannot
faithfully capture the hybrid near-field and far-field channel structures,
leading to degraded estimation performance. This paper introduces DiffPace, a
diffusion-based plug-and-play method for channel estimation. DiffPace uses a
diffusion model (DM) to capture the channel distribution based on the hybrid
spherical and planar-wave (HPSM) model. By applying the plug-and-play approach,
it leverages the DM as prior knowledge, improving CE accuracy. Moreover, DM
performs inference by solving an ordinary differential equation, minimizing the
number of required inference steps compared with stochastic sampling method.
Experimental results show that DiffPace achieves competitive CE performance,
attaining -15 dB normalized mean square error (NMSE) at a signal-to-noise ratio
(SNR) of 10 dB, with 90\% fewer inference steps compared to state-of-the-art
schemes, simultaneously providing high estimation precision and enhanced
computational efficiency.

</details>

along with rich contextual metadata. To explore its utility, we introduce

from EEGNet models trained on clinical data and enriches them with contextual
autoencoder embeddings, followed by unsupervised clustering of patients based

meaningful stratification. Beyond algorithmic performance, we emphasize
